Source Code

These source-code files were derived originally from the scan from MIT's Dibner Institute's now-discontinued website titled "History of Recent Science and Technology", which in turn was originally created by Gary Neff, though his high-quality scans were unfortunately reduced in legibility when presented online. The markings on the front of the printout imply that it was the original AGC developer Norm Brodeur's copy. A scan by Ron Burkey has superceded it, made from a more-legible copy from the collection of original AGC developer Fred Martin. The source code was transcribed from those images by Ron Burkey. Note that the page images presented online are of reduced quality, and that higher-quality images are available. Report any conversion errors or legibility problems in page images to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	ASSEMBLE REVISION 249 OF AGC PROGRAM COLOSSUS BY NASA 2021111-041
	20'35 OCT. 28,1968
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision.

Page 304 

012910,000039:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME -- KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
012911,000040:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO -- 4           DATE -- 27 APRIL 1967           ASSEMBLY -- PINDISK REV 17
012912,000041:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY -- FILENE
012913,000042:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION -- PINBALL GAME BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
012914,000043: 
012915,000044:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
012916,000045: 
012917,000046:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
012918,000047:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
012919,000048:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
012920,000049:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAM, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
012921,000050: 
012922,000051:                                                                                                  #  THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
012923,000052:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
012924,000053:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
012925,000054:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
012926,000055:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
012927,000056: 
012928,000057:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
012929,000058:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS (THESE
012930,000059:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
012931,000060:                                                                                                  #  `EXTENDED VERBS').
012932,000061: 
012933,000062:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION `ASSEMBLY AND 
012934,000063:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION'.
012935,000064: 
012936,000065:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES --
012937,000066: 
012938,000067:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
012939,000068:                                                                                                  #  EACH DEPRESSION OF A MAIN (NAVIGATION) KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES
012940,000069:                                                                                                  #  INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1 (KEYRUPT2) AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO 
012941,000070:                                                                                                  #  CHANNEL 15 (CHANNEL 16).  KEYRUPT1 (KEYRUPT2) PLACES THE KEY
012942,000071:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
012943,000072:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT `CHARIN'), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
012944,000073: 
012945,000074:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
012946,000075:                                                                                                  #  EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT, WHICH
012947,000076:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
012948,000077:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT `CHARIN') AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
012949,000078: 
012950,000079:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
012951,000080:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT `NVSUB' WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
012952,000081:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
012953,000082:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE `NVSUB' AND `NVSBWAIT' (SEE
012954,000083:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
012955,000084: 
012956,000085:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES --
012957,000086: 
012958,000087:                                                                                                  #        IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
012959,000088:                                                                                                  #                1)      ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.

Page 305 

012961,000090:                                                                                                  #                2)      EXTENDED VERBS TO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE
012962,000091:                                                                                                  #                        PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
012963,000092:                                                                                                  #                        RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTEDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
012964,000093:                                                                                                  #                        CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AD DO AN ENDOFJOB.
012965,000094:                                                                                                  #                        ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB.  EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
012966,000095:                                                                                                  #                3)      VERB 37.  CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS `V37' IN THE
012967,000096:                                                                                                  #                        SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
012968,000097:                                                                                                  #                        30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
012969,000098:                                                                                                  #                4)      KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS `PINBRNCH' IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
012970,000099:                                                                                                  #                        ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
012971,000100:                                                                                                  #                        THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND `CADRSTOR' IS NOT 40.
012972,000101: 
012973,000102:                                                                                                  #  IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
012974,000103:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
012975,000104:                                                                                                  #  `NVSUB' AND `NVSBWAIT' (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
012976,000105: 
012977,000106:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES --
012978,000107: 
012979,000108:                                                                                                  #        EXTERNAL INITIATION:
012980,000109:                                                                                                  #                IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
012981,000110:                                                                                                  #                ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO `ENDOFJOB'.
012982,000111: 
012983,000112:                                                                                                  #        INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
012984,000113:                                                                                                  #                IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
012985,000114:                                                                                                  #                (WITH OCTAL 01501).
012986,000115:                                                                                                  #                IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
012987,000116:                                                                                                  #                CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206).  THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
012988,000117:                                                                                                  #                1)      ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
012989,000118:                                                                                                  #                2)      NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
012990,000119: 
012991,000120:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
012992,000121:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
012993,000122: 
012994,000123:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT --
012995,000124: 
012996,000125:                                                                                                  #  INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE `DSPTAB'
012997,000126:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL).  `DSPOUT' (A PART OF T4RUPT)
012998,000127:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE `DSPTAB' INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
012999,000128:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
013000,000129: 
013001,000130:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION --
013002,000131: 
013003,000132:                                                                                                  #  FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
013004,000133:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN `STARTSUB'.  REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
013005,000134:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
013006,000135:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
013007,000136:

Page 306 

013009,000138:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR
013010,000139:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
013011,000140: 
013012,000141:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST --
013013,000142: 
013014,000143:                                                                                                  #  REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
013015,000144:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PACE NUMBERS.
013016,000145: 
013017,000146:                                                                                                  #        NVSUB           CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
013018,000147:                                                                                                  #                        OF RELATED INTEREST     NVSBWAIT
013019,000148:                                                                                                  #                                                NVSUBUSY
013020,000149:                                                                                                  #                                                PRENVBSY
013021,000150: 
013022,000151:                                                                                                  #        ENDIDLE         ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO TO SLEEP WHILE
013023,000152:                                                                                                  #                        AWAITING OPERATOR'S RESPONSE.
013024,000153: 
013025,000154:                                                                                                  #        DSPMM           ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
013026,000155:                                                                                                  #                        PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHT
013027,000156:                                                                                                  #                        (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
013028,000157:                                                                                                  #                        FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
013029,000158: 
013030,000159:                                                                                                  #        BLANKSUB        ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
013031,000160:                                                                                                  #                        COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
013032,000161: 
013033,000162:                                                                                                  #        JAMTERM         ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
013034,000163:                                                                                                  #        JAMPROC         TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V33) FUNCTION.
013035,000164: 
013036,000165:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR         VERBS FOR PERIODIC (1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
013037,000166: 
013038,000167:                                                                                                  #        PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
013039,000168:                                                                                                  #                REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
013040,000169:                                                                                                  #                THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE `NVSUB' (SEE
013041,000170:                                                                                                  #                SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
013042,000171: 
013043,000172:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
013044,000173:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE `DSPABC' (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
013045,000174: 
013046,000175:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION `PINBALL NOUN
013047,000176:                                                                                                  #        TABLES'.
013048,000177: 
013049,000178:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
013050,000179:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
013051,000180:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
013052,000181:                                                                                                  #  (Note that this doc by Green and Filene is/was available online at
013053,000182:                                                                                                  #  http://hrst.mit.edu/hrs/apollo/public/archive/1706.pdf --- RSB 6/2004.)
013054,000183: 
013055,000184:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING QUOTATION IS PROVIDED THROUGH THE COURTESY OF THE AUTHORS.
013056,000185: 
013057,000186:                                                                                                  #        "IT WILL BE PROVED TO THY FACE THAT THOU HAST MEN ABOUT THEE THAT

Page 307 

013059,000188:                                                                                                  #        USUALLY TALK OF A NOUN AND A VERB, AND SUCH ABOMINABLE WORDS AS NO
013060,000189:                                                                                                  #        CHRISTIAN EAR CAN ENDURE TO HEAR."
013061,000190:                                                                                                  #                                        HENRY 6, ACT 2, SCENE 4
013062,000191: 
013063,000192:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ASSIGNMENTS FOR PINBALL ARE MADE ELSEWHERE
013064,000193: 
013065,000194:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
013066,000195: 
013067,000196:                                                                                                  # DSPCOUNT       ERASE                   # DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
013068,000197:                                                                                                  # DECBRNCH       ERASE                   # +DEC, -DEC, OCT INDICATOR
013069,000198:                                                                                                  # VERBREG        ERASE                   # VERB CODE
013070,000199:                                                                                                  # NOUNREG        ERASE                   # NOUN CODE
013071,000200:                                                                                                  # XREG           ERASE                   # R1 INPUT BUFFER
013072,000201:                                                                                                  # YREG           ERASE                   # R2 INPUT BUFFER
013073,000202:                                                                                                  # ZREG           ERASE                   # R3 INPUT BUFFER
013074,000203:                                                                                                  # XREGLP         ERASE                   # LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
013075,000204:                                                                                                  # YREGLP         ERASE                   # LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
013076,000205:                                                                                                  # HITEMOUT       =       YREGLP          # TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS,MIN,SEC
013077,000206:                                                                                                  #                                        # MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
013078,000207:                                                                                                  # ZREGLP         ERASE                   # LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
013079,000208:                                                                                                  # LOTEMOUT       =       ZREGLP          # TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS,MIN,SEC
013080,000209:                                                                                                  #                                        # MUST = HITEMOUT+1
013081,000210:                                                                                                  # MODREG         ERASE                   # MODE CODE
013082,000211:                                                                                                  # DSPLOCK        ERASE                   # KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
013083,000212:                                                                                                  # REQRET         ERASE                   # RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
013084,000213:                                                                                                  # LOADSTAT       ERASE                   # STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
013085,000214:                                                                                                  # CLPASS         ERASE                   # PASS INDICATOR FOR CLEAR
013086,000215:                                                                                                  # NOUT           ERASE                   # ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
013087,000216:                                                                                                  # NOUNCADR       ERASE                   # MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
013088,000217:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE        ERASE                   # N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
013089,000218:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE1       ERASE                   # NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR (MATBS1) = MONSAVE+1
013090,000219:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE2       ERASE                   # NVMONOPT OPTIONS
013091,000220:                                                                                                  # DSPTAB         ERASE   +13D            # 0-10, DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER 11-13, C RELAYS.
013092,000221:                                                                                                  # CADRSTOR       ERASE                   # ENDIDLE STORAGE
013093,000222:                                                                                                  # NVQTEM         ERASE                   # NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
013094,000223:                                                                                                  #                                        # MUST = NVBNKTEM-1.
013095,000224:                                                                                                  # NVBNKTEM       ERASE                   # NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
013096,000225:                                                                                                  #                                        # MUST = NVQTEM+1
013097,000226:                                                                                                  # VERBSAVE       ERASE                   # NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
013098,000227:                                                                                                  # DSPLIST        ERASE                   # WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
013099,000228:                                                                                                  # EXTVBACT       ERASE                   # EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
013100,000229:                                                                                                  # DSPTEM1        ERASE   +2              # BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
013101,000230:                                                                                                  # DSPTEM2        ERASE   +2              # BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
013102,000231: 
013103,000232:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION.
013104,000233: 
013105,000234:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION

Page 308 

013107,000236:                                                                                                  # DSEXIT         =       INTB15+         # RETURN FOR DSPIN
013108,000237:                                                                                                  # EXITEM         =       INTB15+         # RETURN FOR SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE SELECT
013109,000238:                                                                                                  # BLANKRET       =       INTB15+         # RETURN FOR 2BLANK
013110,000239:                                                                                                  # WRDRET         =       INTBIT15        # RETURN FOR 5BLANK.
013111,000240:                                                                                                  # WDRET          =       INTBIT15        # RETURN FOR DSPWD
013112,000241:                                                                                                  # DECRET         =       INTBIT15        # RETURN FOR PUTCOM(DEC LOAD)
013113,000242:                                                                                                  # 21/22REG       =       INTBIT15        # TEMP FOR CHARIN
013114,000243:                                                                                                  # UPDATRET       =       POLISH          # RETURN FOR UPDATNN, UPDATVB
013115,000244:                                                                                                  # CHAR           =       POLISH          # TEMP FOR CHARIN
013116,000245:                                                                                                  # ERCNT          =       POLISH          # COUNTER FOR ERROR LIGHT RESET
013117,000246:                                                                                                  # DECOUNT        =       POLISH          # COUNTER FOR SCALING AND DISPLAY (DEC)
013118,000247:                                                                                                  # SGNON          =       VBUF            # TEMP FOR +,- ON
013119,000248:                                                                                                  # NOUNTEM        =       VBUF            # COUNTER FOR MIXNOUN FETCH
013120,000249:                                                                                                  # DISTEM         =       VBUF            # COUNTER FOR OCTAL DISPLAY VERB
013121,000250:                                                                                                  # DECTEM         =       VBUF            # COUNTER FOR FETCH (DEC DISPLAY VERBS)
013122,000251:                                                                                                  # SGNOFF         =       VBUF +1         # TEMP FOR +,- ON
013123,000252:                                                                                                  # NVTEMP         =       VBUF +1         # TEMP FOR NVSUB
013124,000253:                                                                                                  # SFTEMP1        =       VBUF +1         # STORAGE FOR SF CONST HI PART (=SFTEMP2-1)
013125,000254:                                                                                                  # HITEMIN        =       VBUF +1         # TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS,MIN,SEC
013126,000255:                                                                                                  #                                        # MUST = LOTEMIN-1.
013127,000256:                                                                                                  # CODE           =       VBUF +2         # FOR DSPIN
013128,000257:                                                                                                  # SFTEMP2        =       VBUF +2         # STORAGE FOR SF CONST LO PART (=SFTEMP1+1)
013129,000258:                                                                                                  # LOTEMIN        =       VBUF +2         # TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS,MIN,SEC
013130,000259:                                                                                                  #                                        # MUST = HITEMIN+1
013131,000260:                                                                                                  # MIXTEMP        =       VBUF +3         # FOR MIXNOUN DATA
013132,000261:                                                                                                  # SIGNRET        =       VBUF +3         # RETURN FOR +,- ON
013133,000262:                                                                                                  #  ALSO MIXTEMP+1 = VBUF+4, MIXTEMP+2 = VBUF+5
013134,000263:                                                                                                  # ENTRET         =       DOTINC          # EXIT FROM ENTER
013135,000264:                                                                                                  # WDONT          =       DOTRET          # CHAR COUNTER FOR DSPWD
013136,000265:                                                                                                  # INREL          =       DOTRET          # INPUT BUFFER SELECTION
013137,000266:                                                                                                  # DSPMMTEM       =       MATINC          # DSPCOUNT SAVE FOR DSPMM
013138,000267:                                                                                                  # MIXBR          =       MATINC          # INDICATOR FOR MIXED OR NORMAL NOUN
013139,000268:                                                                                                  # TEM1           ERASE                   # EXEC TEMP
013140,000269:                                                                                                  # DSREL          =       TEM1            # REL ADDRESS FOR DSPIN
013141,000270:                                                                                                  # TEM2           ERASE                   # EXEC TEMP
013142,000271:                                                                                                  # DSMAG          =       TEM2            # MAGNITUDE STORE FOR DSPIN
013143,000272:                                                                                                  # IDADDTEM       =       TEM2            # MIXNOUN INDIRECT ADDRESS (garbled)
013144,000273:                                                                                                  # TEM3           ERASE                   # EXEC TEMP
013145,000274:                                                                                                  # COUNT          =       TEM3            # FOR DSPIN

Page 309 

013147,000276:                                                                                                  # TEM4           ERASE                   # EXEC TEMP
013148,000277:                                                                                                  # LSTPTR         =       TEM4            # LIST POINTER FOR GRABUST
013149,000278:                                                                                                  # RELRET         =       TEM4            # RETURN FOR RELDSP
013150,000279:                                                                                                  # FREERET        =       TEM4            # RETURN FOR FREEDSP
013151,000280:                                                                                                  # DSPWDRET       =       TEM4            # RETURN FOR DSPSIGN
013152,000281:                                                                                                  # SEPSCRET       =       TEM4            # RETURN FOR SEPSEC
013153,000282:                                                                                                  # SEPMNRET       =       TEM4            # RETURN FOR SEPMIN
013154,000283:                                                                                                  # TEM5           ERASE                   # EXEC TEMP
013155,000284:                                                                                                  # NOUNADD        =       TEM5            # TEMP STORAGE FOR NOUN ADDRESS
013156,000285:                                                                                                  # NNADTEM        ERASE                   # TEMP FOR NOUN ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY
013157,000286:                                                                                                  # NNTYPTEM       ERASE                   # TEMP FOR NOUN TYPE TABLE ENTRY
013158,000287:                                                                                                  # IDAD1TEM       ERASE                   # TEMP FOR INDIR ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
013159,000288:                                                                                                  #                                        # MUST = IDAD2TEM-1, = IDAD3TEM-2
013160,000289:                                                                                                  # IDAD2TEM       ERASE                   # TEMP FOR INDIR ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
013161,000290:                                                                                                  #                                        # MUST = IDAD1TEM+1, IDAD3TEM-1.
013162,000291:                                                                                                  # IDAD3TEM       ERASE                   # TEMP FOR INDIR ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
013163,000292:                                                                                                  #                                        # MUST = IDAD1TEM+2, IDAD2TEM+1.
013164,000293:                                                                                                  # RUTMXTEM       ERASE                   # TEMP FOR SF ROUT TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN ONLY)
013165,000294: 
013166,000295:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION.
013167,000296: 
013168,000297:                                                                                                  #  ADDITIONAL TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
013169,000298: 
013170,000299:                                                                                                  #        MPAC, THRU MPAC +6
013171,000300:                                                                                                  #        BUF, +1, +2
013172,000301:                                                                                                  #        BUF2, +1, +2
013173,000302:                                                                                                  #        MPTEMP
013174,000303:                                                                                                  #        ADDRWD
013175,000304: 
013176,000305:                                                                                                  #  END OF ADDITIONAL TEMPS FOR PINBALL EXEC ACTION
013177,000306: 
013178,000307:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013179,000308: 
013180,000309:                                                                                                  # DSPCNT         ERASE                   # COUNTER FOR DSPOUT
013181,000310:                                                                                                  # UPLOCK         ERASE                   # BIT1 = UPLINK INTERLOCK (ACTIVATED BY
013182,000311:                                                                                                  #                                        # RECEPTION OF A BAD MESSAGE IN UPLINK)
013183,000312: 
013184,000313:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013185,000314: 
013186,000315:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013187,000316: 
013188,000317:                                                                                                  # KEYTEMP1       =       WAITEXIT        # TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
013189,000318:                                                                                                  # DSRUPTEM       =       WAITEXIT        # TEMP FOR DSPOUT
013190,000319:                                                                                                  # KEYTEMP2       =       RUPTAGN         # TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
013191,000320: 
013192,000321:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013193,000322:

Page 310 

013195,000324:                                                                                                  #  THE INPUT CODES ASSUMED FOR THE KEYBOARD ARE,
013196,000325:                                                                                                  #        0               10000
013197,000326:                                                                                                  #        1               00001
013198,000327:                                                                                                  #        9               01001
013199,000328:                                                                                                  #        VERB            10001
013200,000329:                                                                                                  #        ERROR RES       10010
013201,000330:                                                                                                  #        KEY RLSE        11001
013202,000331:                                                                                                  #        +               11010
013203,000332:                                                                                                  #        -               11011
013204,000333:                                                                                                  #        ENTER           11100
013205,000334:                                                                                                  #        CLEAR           11110
013206,000335:                                                                                                  #        NOUN            11111
013207,000336: 
013208,000337:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL.  SET OUT0 TO AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
013209,000338:                                                                                                  #  A'S   SELECTS A RELAYWORD.  THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
013210,000339:                                                                                                  #        ENERGIZED.
013211,000340:                                                                                                  #  B     FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
013212,000341:                                                                                                  #  C'S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
013213,000342:                                                                                                  #  D'S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
013214,000343: 
013215,000344:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
013216,000345:                                                                                                  #        MD1             MD2 (MAJOR MODE)
013217,000346:                                                                                                  #        VD1             VD2 (VERB)                      ND1             ND2 (NOUN)
013218,000347:                                                                                                  #        R1D1            R1D2            R1D3            R1D4            R1D5 (R1)
013219,000348:                                                                                                  #        R2D1            R2D2            R2D3            R2D4            R2D5 (R2)
013220,000349:                                                                                                  #        R3D1            R3D2            R3D3            R3D4            R3D5 (R3)
013221,000350: 
013222,000351:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
013223,000352: 
013224,000353:                                                                                                  #        MD1     25              R2D1    11              ALL ARE OCTAL
013225,000354:                                                                                                  #        MD2     24              R2D2    10
013226,000355:                                                                                                  #        VD1     23              R2D3    7
013227,000356:                                                                                                  #        VD2     22              R2D4    6
013228,000357:                                                                                                  #        ND1     21              R2D5    5
013229,000358:                                                                                                  #        ND2     20              R3D1    4
013230,000359:                                                                                                  #        R1D1    16              R3D2    3
013231,000360:                                                                                                  #        R1D2    15              R3D3    2
013232,000361:                                                                                                  #        R1D3    14              R3D4    1
013233,000362:                                                                                                  #        R1D4    13              R3D5    0
013234,000363:                                                                                                  #        R1D5    12
013235,000364: 
013236,000365:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11-REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
013237,000366: 
013238,000367:                                                                                                  #        DSPTAB          RELAYWD         BIT11           BITS 10-6       BITS 5-1
013239,000368:                                                                                                  #        RELADD
013240,000369:                                                                                                  #        10              1011                            MD1 (25)        MD2 (24)
013241,000370:                                                                                                  #        9               1010                            VD1 (23)        VD2 (22)
013242,000371:                                                                                                  #        8               1001                            ND1 (21)        ND2 (20)
013243,000372:                                                                                                  #        7               1000                                            R1D1 (16)

Page 311 

013245,000374:                                                                                                  #        6               0111            +R1             R1D2 (15)       R1D3 (14)
013246,000375:                                                                                                  #        5               0110            -R1             R1D4 (13)       R1D5 (12)
013247,000376:                                                                                                  #        4               0101            +R2             R2D1 (11)       R2D2 (10)
013248,000377:                                                                                                  #        3               0100            -R2             R2D3 (7)        R2D4 (6)
013249,000378:                                                                                                  #        2               0011                            R2D5 (5)        R3D1 (4)
013250,000379:                                                                                                  #        1               0010            +R3             R3D2 (3)        R3D3 (2)
013251,000380:                                                                                                  #        0               0001            -R3             R3D4 (1)        R3D5 (0)
013252,000381:                                                                                                  #                        0000        NO RELAYWORD
013253,000382: 
013254,000383:                                                                                                  #  THE 5-BIT OUTOUT RELAY CODES ARE:
013255,000384: 
013256,000385:                                                                                                  #        BLANK   00000
013257,000386:                                                                                                  #        0       10101
013258,000387:                                                                                                  #        1       00011
013259,000388:                                                                                                  #        2       11001
013260,000389:                                                                                                  #        3       11011
013261,000390:                                                                                                  #        4       01111
013262,000391:                                                                                                  #        5       11110
013263,000392:                                                                                                  #        6       11100
013264,000393:                                                                                                  #        7       10011
013265,000394:                                                                                                  #        8       11101
013266,000395:                                                                                                  #        9       11111
013267,000396: 
013268,000397:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT BITS USED BY PINBALL:
013269,000398: 
013270,000399:                                                                                                  #        KEY RELEASE LIGHT       --      BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11
013271,000400:                                                                                                  #        VERB/NOUN FLASH         --      BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
013272,000401:                                                                                                  #        OPERATOR ERROR LIGHT    --      BIT 7 OF CHANNEL 11
013273,000402:

013346,000475: 
013347,000476:                                                                                                  #  NUM ASSEMBLES OCTAL 3 BITS AT A TIME.  FOR DECIMAL IT CONVERTS INCOMING
013348,000477:                                                                                                  #  WORD AS A FRACTION, KEEPING RESULTS TO DP.
013349,000478:                                                                                                  #  OCTAL RESULTS ARE LEFT IN XREG, YREG, OR ZREG.  HI PART OF DEC IN XREG,
013350,000479:                                                                                                  #  YREG, ZREG.  THE LOW PARTS IN XREGLP, YREGLP, OR ZREGLP.

013672,000801:                                                                                                  #  ENTER PASS 0 IS THE EXECUTE FUNCTION.  HIGHER ORDER ENTERS ARE TO LOAD
013673,000802:                                                                                                  #  DATA.  THE SIGN OF REQRET DETERMINES THE PASS, + FOR PASS 0, - FOR HIGHER
013674,000803:                                                                                                  #  PASSES
013675,000804: 
013676,000805:                                                                                                  #  MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED (MCTBS) NOUNS DESIRE AN ECADR TO BE LOADED
013677,000806:                                                                                                  #  WHEN USED WITH LOAD VERBS, MONITOR VERBS, OR DISPLAY VERBS (EXCEPT
013678,000807:                                                                                                  #  VERB = FIXED MEMORY DISPLAY, WHICH REQUIRES AN FCADR).

013961,001090:

Page 327 

013963,001092:                                                                                                  #  NOUN TABLES
013964,001093: 
013965,001094:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
013966,001095:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE ECADR FOR EACH NOUN.
013967,001096:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.  - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR (E OR F) TO
013968,001097:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED.  -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED.  -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
013969,001098:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
013970,001099: 
013971,001100:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS (IDADDREL) IN LOW
013972,001101:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
013973,001102: 
013974,001103:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
013975,001104: 
013976,001105:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE,  M'S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
013977,001106:                                                                                                  #                        N'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
013978,001107:                                                                                                  #                        P'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
013979,001108: 
013980,001109:                                                                                                  #  MIXED-CASE,           M'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER    3 COMPONENT CASE
013981,001110:                                                                                                  #                        N'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
013982,001111:                                                                                                  #                        P'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
013983,001112:                                                                                                  #                        N'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER    2 COMPONENT CASE
013984,001113:                                                                                                  #                        P'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
013985,001114:                                                                                                  #                        P'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER    1 COMPONENT CASE
013986,001115: 
013987,001116:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE (IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY
013988,001117:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.  IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
013989,001118:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
013990,001119: 
013991,001120:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABEL FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
013992,001121:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
013993,001122: 
013994,001123:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE (RUTMXTAB) FOR MIXED
013995,001124:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY.  THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN.  THE FORM IS,
013996,001125: 
013997,001126:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
013998,001127: 
013999,001128:                                                                                                  #  Q'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER          3 COMPONENT CASE
014000,001129:                                                                                                  #  R'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
014001,001130:                                                                                                  #  S'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
014002,001131:                                                                                                  #  R'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER          2 COMPONENT CASE
014003,001132:                                                                                                  #  S'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
014004,001133: 
014005,001134:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
014006,001135:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMONENTS IN NOUN.
014007,001136:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
014008,001137: 
014009,001138:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
014010,001139:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED.  ALARM IF VIOLATION.
014011,001140: 
014012,001141:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
014013,001142:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER.  IF NOT, ALARM.
014014,001143:

Page 328 

014016,001145:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAY VERBS
014017,001146: 
014018,001147: 41,2352           44711        DSPABC             CS       TWO                                   
014019,001148: 41,2353           02423                           TC       COMPTEST

014526,001655:                                                                                                  #  THIS IS A SPECIAL PURPOS VERB FOR DISPLAYING A DOUBLE PRECISION AGC
014527,001656:                                                                                                  #  WORD AS 10 DECIMAL DIGITS ON THE AGC DISPLAY PANEL.  IT CAN BE USED WITH
014528,001657:                                                                                                  #  ANY NOUN, EXCEPT MIXED NOUNS.  IT DISPLAYS THE CONTENTS
014529,001658:                                                                                                  #  OF THE REGISTER NOUNADD IS POINTING TO.  IF USED WITH NOUNS WHICH ARE
014530,001659:                                                                                                  #  INHERENTLY NOT DP SUCH AS THE CDU COUNTERS THE DISPLAY WILL BE GARBAGE.
014531,001660:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAY IS IN R1 AND R2 ONLY WITH THE SIGN IN R1.

Page 351 

015125,002254:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY.  IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
015126,002255:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
015127,002256:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
015128,002257:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
015129,002258:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
015130,002259: 
015131,002260:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION.
015132,002261:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET.  IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
015133,002262:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE.  IT SAVES
015134,002263:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED.  BIT 15 OF
015135,002264:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT).  BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
015136,002265:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
015137,002266:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT).  IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KIMONON.
015138,002267: 
015139,002268:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON (+=ON, +0=OFF)
015140,002269:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
015141,002270:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
015142,002271: 
015143,002272:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
015144,002273:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
015145,002274: 
015146,002275:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
015147,002276:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
015148,002277: 
015149,002278:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOESN'T TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW.
015150,002279:

015278,002407: 
015279,002408:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
015280,002409:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED.  THE FCADR OF THE 
015281,002410:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN.  IT HANDLES F/F (FCADR 4000-7777)
015282,002411:                                                                                                  #  
015283,002412:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
015284,002413: 
015285,002414:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
015286,002415:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
015287,002416:                                                                                                  #        V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
015288,002417: 
015289,002418:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
015290,002419:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                             V27N01E(FCADR)E
015291,002420:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,     V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E     V27N01E(FCADR)E
015292,002421: 
015293,002422: 41,3343           34333        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
015294,002423: 41,3344           54777                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
015295,002424: 41,3345           31047                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
015296,002425: 41,3346           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
015297,002426: 41,3347           31017                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
015298,002427: 41,3350           04610                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.
