015717,002846:                                                                                                  #  END OF LOAD.

Page 364 

015719,002848: 
015720,002849:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
015721,002850: 
015722,002851:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
015723,002852: 
015724,002853:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
015725,002854:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
015726,002855:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
015727,002856:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
015728,002857: 
015729,002858:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
015730,002859:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
015731,002860:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
015732,002861: 
015733,002862:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
015734,002863:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
015735,002864:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
015736,002865:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
015737,002866:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
015738,002867:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
015739,002868:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES.  HITTING KEYRLSE WILL
015740,002869:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEOFRE HE OBSCURED
015741,002870:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST.  THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
015742,002871:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARET'S DISPLAY
015743,002872:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
015744,002873: 
015745,002874: 40,3362           44710        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
015746,002875: 40,3363           00006                           EXTEND                                         
015747,002876: 40,3364           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OF UPACT LITE
015748,002877: 40,3365           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
015749,002878: 40,3366           34675                           CAF      BIT14                                 
015750,002879: 40,3367           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
015751,002880: 40,3370           10000                           CCS      A                                     
015752,002881: 40,3371           03400                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND,
015753,002882: 40,3372           04473        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR
015754,002883: 40,3373           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
015755,002884: 40,3374           03376                           TC       +2                                    #        DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
015756,002885: 40,3375           05112                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
015757,002886: 40,3376           04574                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
015758,002887: 40,3377           21176                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
015759,002888: 40,3400           34714        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
015760,002889: 40,3401           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #        JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
015761,002890: 40,3402           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
015762,002891: 40,3403           05112                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #        CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
015763,002892: 40,3404           04516                           TC       RELDSP1                               
015764,002893: 40,3405           05112                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
015765,002894: 
015766,002895: 40,3406                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
015767,002896:

Page 365 

015769,002898:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUBROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER.  IT CAN BE
015770,002899:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
015771,002900:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
015772,002901:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
015773,002902:                                                                                                  #  V'S ARE THE 7-BIT VERB CODE.  N'S ARE THE 7-BIT NOUN CODE.
015774,002903: 
015775,002904:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WTIH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
015776,002905:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS ---
015777,002906:                                                                                                  #  -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R'S ONLY.
015778,002907: 
015779,002908:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WTIH MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
015780,002909:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
015781,002910: 
015782,002911:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
015783,002912:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAIALBLE.  THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
015784,002913:                                                                                                  #  IF V'S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
015785,002914:                                                                                                  #  ACTION).  IF N'S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO
015786,002915:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
015787,002916: 
015788,002917:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
015789,002918:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
015790,002919:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
015791,002920:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
015792,002921: 
015793,002922:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
015794,002923:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET.
015795,002924:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
015796,002925:                                                                                                  #  PROCED WITOHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
015797,002926:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
015798,002927:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
015799,002928:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
015800,002929: 
015801,002930:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
015802,002931:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AND EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR).
015803,002932: 
015804,002933:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
015805,002934:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
015806,002935: 
015807,002936:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
015808,002937:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
015809,002938: 
015810,002939:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR `PLEASE PERFORM' SITUATIONS
015811,002940:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK).  FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
015812,002941:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THEREGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
015813,002942:                                                                                                  #  `CHECKLIST' NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE `CHECKLIST'
015814,002943:                                                                                                  #  NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WTIH THE `PLEASE PERFORM' VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
015815,002944:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS.  THIS `PASTES UP' THE `PLEASE PERFORM' VERB INTO THE VERB
015816,002945:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
015817,002946: 
015818,002947:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 366 

015820,002949:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L.  IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
015821,002950:                                                                                                  #  A.  AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASED INT THE VERB
015822,002951:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
015823,002952:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L.  IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
015824,002953:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS.  (THIS VERB
015825,002954:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.)  IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
015826,002955:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED BO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
015827,002956:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB.  IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
015828,002957:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
015829,002958: 
015830,002959:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
015831,002960:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET.  (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)

015833,002962:    4170                                           SETLOC   ENDALM     +1

015835,002964:    4170                                           COUNT    02/PIN

015948,003077:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR BIT.

015950,003079: 
015951,003080:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      +0      INACTIVE (WAITING FOR DATA).  SET BY NVSUB
015952,003081:                                                                                                  #                +1      PROCEED NO DATA.  SET BY SPECIAL VERB
015953,003082:                                                                                                  #                -1      TERMINATE.  SET BY SPECIAL VERB.
015954,003083:                                                                                                  #                -0      DATA IN.  SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE.
015955,003084:                                                                                                  #                        OR RESEQUENCE.  SET BY VERB 32
015956,003085: 
015957,003086:                                                                                                  #  L TO ENDIDLE (FIXED FIXED).
015958,003087:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
015959,003088:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED.  ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
015960,003089:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
015961,003090:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOB SLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
015962,003091:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
015963,003092:                                                                                                  #        L+1     FOR TERMINATE
015964,003093:                                                                                                  #        L+2     FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
015965,003094:                                                                                                  #        L+3     FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
015966,003095:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DTA.

Page 369 

015968,003097: 
015969,003098:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 1206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP
015970,003099:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL.  IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
015971,003100:                                                                                                  #        1)      CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
015972,003101:                                                                                                  #                EXCEEDED.  (+-NZ INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDDLE.)
015973,003102:                                                                                                  #        2)      DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
015974,003103:                                                                                                  #                NVSUBUSY.
015975,003104: 
015976,003105:    4223           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
015977,003106:    4224           04234                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
015978,003107:    4225           04240                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
015979,003108:    4226           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DON'T SET DSPLOC TO 1 SO CAN USE
015980,003109:    4227           74747                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATE MONITOR.
015981,003110:    4230           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
015982,003111:    4231           55042                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
015983,003112:    4232           05070                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
015984,003113: 
015985,003114:    4233           05112        ENDINST            TC       ENDOFJOB                              
015986,003115:

016313,003442:

Page 377 

016315,003444:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM.
016316,003445: 
016317,003446:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
016318,003447:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR.  THE OLD CRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
016319,003448:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
016320,003449:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
016321,003450: 
016322,003451:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY TEH KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
016323,003452:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.      1)      BY ENDIDLE
016324,003453:                                                                                                  #                2)      BY NVSUBUSY
016325,003454:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERITTED ASLEEP VIA
016326,003455:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME.  IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
016327,003456:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY AJOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
016328,003457:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
016329,003458: 
016330,003459:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
016331,003460:                                                                                                  #                        CAF             V/N
016332,003461:                                                                                                  #        L               TC              NVSUB
016333,003462:                                                                                                  #        L+1             RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
016334,003463:                                                                                                  #        L+2             RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
016335,003464: 
016336,003465:                                                                                                  #  A ROUTINE CALLED NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL) TO PUT
016337,003466:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
016338,003467:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM.  NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
016339,003468:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
016340,003469:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
016341,003470: 
016342,003471:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
016343,003472:                                                                                                  #        CAF     WAKEFCADR
016344,003473:                                                                                                  #        TC      NVSUBUSY
016345,003474: 
016346,003475:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
016347,003476:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION).  IT IS
016348,003477:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
016349,003478:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
016350,003479: 
016351,003480:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
016352,003481:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL.  IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MAKE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
016353,003482:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
016354,003483: 
016355,003484:                                                                                                  #        1)      DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY FO THE DSPLIST
016356,003485:                                                                                                  #                IS EXCEEDED.
016357,003486:                                                                                                  #        2)      CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 378 

016359,003488:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE.  (+-NZ INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
016360,003489: 
016361,003490:    4453           44460        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
016362,003491:    4454           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF (LOC
016363,003492:    4455           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
016364,003493:    4456           04574        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
016365,003494:    4457           10550                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
016366,003495:    4460           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
016367,003496: 
016368,003497:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
016369,003498:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
016370,003499: 
016371,003500: 04,2550                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
016372,003501: 04,2550                                           COUNT    07/PIN                                
016373,003502: 
016374,003503: 04,2550           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
016375,003504: 04,2551           04234                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
016376,003505: 04,2552           04240                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
016377,003506: 04,2553           04410                           TC       RELDSPON                              
016378,003507: 04,2554           30001                           CA       L                                     
016379,003508: 04,2555           55043                           TS       DSPLIST                               
016380,003509: 04,2556           05070        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
016381,003510: 
016382,003511:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
016383,003512:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
016384,003513:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE).  IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
016385,003514:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
016386,003515:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
016387,003516: 
016388,003517:    4461                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
016389,003518:    4461                                           COUNT    02/PIN                                
016390,003519: 
016391,003520:    4461           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
016392,003521:    4462           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
016393,003522:    4463           34675                           CAF      BIT14                                 
016394,003523:    4464           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
016395,003524:    4465           61012                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
016396,003525:    4466           10000                           CCS      A                                     
016397,003526:    4467           14471                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
016398,003527:    4470           14200                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
016399,003528:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
016400,003529:    4471           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2.  PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
016401,003530:    4472           14453                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
016402,003531: 
016403,003532:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
016404,003533:                                                                                                  #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
016405,003534: 
016406,003535:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.
016407,003536: 
016408,003537:    4473           56002        RELDSP             XCH      Q                                     #  SET DSPLOCK TO +0, TURN RELDSP LIGHT

Page 379 

016410,003539:    4474           54144                           TS       RELRET                                #  OFF, SEARCH DSPLIST
016411,003540:    4475           44675                           CS       BIT14                                 
016412,003541:    4476           00004                           INHINT                                         
016413,003542:    4477           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              
016414,003543:    4500           55021                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
016415,003544:    4501           11043                           CCS      DSPLIST                               
016416,003545:    4502           04504                           TC       +2                                    
016417,003546:    4503           04507                           TC       RELDSP2                               #  LIST EMPTY
016418,003547:    4504           34714                           CAF      ZERO                                  
016419,003548:    4505           57043                           XCH      DSPLIST                               
016420,003549:    4506           05074                           TC       JOBWAKE                               
016421,003550:    4507           00003        RELDSP2            RELINT                                         
016422,003551:    4510           44706                           CS       BIT5                                  #  TURN OFF KEY RELEASE LIGHT
016423,003552:    4511           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  (BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11)
016424,003553:    4512           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              
016425,003554:    4513           34714                           CAF      ZERO                                  
016426,003555:    4514           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK                               
016427,003556:    4515           00144                           TC       RELRET                                
016428,003557:    4516           56002        RELDSP1            XCH      Q                                     #  SET DSPLOCK TO +0.  NO DSPLIST SEARCH.
016429,003558:    4517           54144                           TS       RELRET                                #  TURN KEY RLSE LIGHT OFF IF DSPLIST IS
016430,003559:                                                                                                  #  EMPTY.  LEAVE KEY RLSE LIGHT ALONE IF 
016431,003560:                                                                                                  #  DSPLIST IS NOT EMPTY.

016549,003678:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF:
016550,003679:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
016551,003680:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
016552,003681: 
016553,003682:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
016554,003683:                                                                                                  #  
016555,003684:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROS THE `TEST ALARM' OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY, RESTART.
016556,003685:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS `CAUTION RESET' TO 1.
016557,003686:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.
016558,003687: 
016559,003688: 40,3504                                           SETLOC   DOPROC     +2                         
016560,003689: 40,3504                                           COUNT    40/PIN                                
016561,003690:

016563,003692: 40,3505           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #  LIGHT RESET LEAVES DSPLOCK CHANGED.
016564,003693: 40,3506           00004                           INHINT                                         
016565,003694: 40,3507           34701                           CAF      BIT10                                 #  TURN ON `CAUTION RESET' OUTBIT
016566,003695: 40,3510           00006                           EXTEND                                         
016567,003696: 40,3511           05011                           WOR      DSALMOUT                              #  BIT10 CHAN 11
016568,003697: 40,3512           33572                           CAF      GL+NOATT                              #  LEAVE GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT INTACT,
016569,003698: 40,3513           71036                           MASK     DSPTAB     +11D                       #  TURNING OFF AUTO, HOLD, FREE,
016570,003699: 40,3514           64674                           AD       BIT15                                 #  PROG ALARM, AND TRACKER.

016574,003703: 40,3520           64763                           AD       PRIO16                                #  EXISTS, THE ALARM WILL COME BACK.
